RTV also known as Honda Bond is amazing. You just throw it all over, bolt up, and no more leaks hahahaha
Congratulations on the first start. I will say that you will absolutely want to install the full exhaust system and get the car to an experienced Lamborghini tech with the correct computer. The early cars need to have their throttle bodies calibrated and it can only be done with the computer. As a tip, make sure the calibration is run a number of times. Most techs only do it once but if you run it multiple times it more and more fine tunes the settings and yields a result you can really feel. My tech ran mine 5 times and it was a big difference to drivability and smoothness. Also if you get the computer hooked up they can diagnose a lot of parameters on the engine and make sure it is running correctly. Again awesome work and well done on the engine start milestone.
